		}

	continuous_focus_position = { x = 0 y = 0 }

	shared_focus = GRW_GLA_organizational_meetings

}

									always = yes
								}
							}
						}
					}

								has_country_flag = GRW_Chykchyryn_uprising_flag
							}
						}

									always = yes
								}
							}
						}
					}

					}
					transfer_technology = yes
					set_research_slots = 3

					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = communism
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = GRY_cornilo_khurshevich
						desc = "GRY_CORNBOI_DESC"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/GRY/Cornilo_Khursevich.tga"

					}

					}

					set_war_support = 0.8

					add_ideas = pre_industrial_society2

					}
				}
			}

					}
					every_state = {

shared_focus = {#完成革命使命
	id = GRW_fulfilling_the_revolutionary_mission
	icon = GFX_goal_tfv_burn_the_royal_portraits
	cost = 6
	prerequisite = {
		focus = GRW_southern_griffonia_strategy
	}
	relative_position_id = GRW_southern_griffonia_strategy
	x = 0
	y = 1
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 10
	}
	available = {
		NOT = {
			country_exists = SIC
			country_exists = FAL
			country_exists = WNG
			country_exists = TAL
			country_exists = FRN
			country_exists = ARA
			country_exists = BOI
			country_exists = LAK
		}
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = GRI_empire_rising_flag
			date > 1012.01.01
		}
	}
	bypass = {
		owns_state = 382
	}
	will_lead_to_war_with = GRD
	will_lead_to_war_with = FEA
	will_lead_to_war_with = STW
	will_lead_to_war_with = ANG
	will_lead_to_war_with = PYT
	will_lead_to_war_with = ROU
	will_lead_to_war_with = KAT
	will_lead_to_war_with = BRZ
	will_lead_to_war_with = YAL
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus GRW_fulfilling_the_revolutionary_mission"
		custom_effect_tooltip = GRW_fulfilling_the_revolutionary_mission_tt
		add_state_claim = 382
		if = {
			limit = {
				382 = {
					owner = {
						NOT = {
							original_tag = ROOT
						}
						tag = GRD
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					GRD = {
						has_government = communism
					}
				}
				GRD = {
					add_to_array = {
						array = GRW.revolution_diplomacy
						value = THIS
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				create_wargoal = {
					target = GRD
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			382 = {
				owner = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_government = communism
						}
						add_to_array = {
							array = GRW.revolution_diplomacy
							value = THIS
						}
					}
					else = {
						ROOT = {
							create_wargoal = {
								target = PREV
								type = annex_everything
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = ANG
						original_tag = YAL
						original_tag = PYT
						original_tag = KAT
						original_tag = ROU
						original_tag = GRI
						original_tag = FEA
						original_tag = STW
						original_tag = BRZ
						original_tag = EYR
					}
				}
				add_to_array = {
					array = GRW.revolution_diplomacy
					value = THIS
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
shared_focus = {#修订爱勒海条约
	id = GRW_renegotiate_eler_sea_agreement
	icon = GFX_goal_CTL_h_contacts
	cost = 4
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 10
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = GRW_independent_autonomous_foreign_policy
	}
	relative_position_id = GRW_independent_autonomous_foreign_policy
	x = 1
	y = 1
	available = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = GRW_earlygame_41_flag
		}
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = GRW_eler_sea_agreement_flag
			days > 210
		}
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = GRW_last_agreement_days_tt
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = GRW_eler_sea_agreement_flag
				days > 210
			}
		}
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = GRW_renegotiate_eler_sea_agreement_tt
			OR = {
				has_idea = GRW_talk_with_MCW_idea1
				AND = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = GRW_talk_with_MCW_idea2
						has_idea = GRW_talk_with_MCW_idea4
					}
					check_variable = {
						resource_produced@oil > 45
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus GRW_renegotiate_eler_sea_agreement"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = GRW_talk_with_MCW_idea1
			}
			add_political_power = -50
			add_stability = 0.04
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.03
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						resource_produced@oil > 45
					}
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GRW_talk_with_MCW_idea1
					add_idea = GRW_talk_with_MCW_idea3
				}
				MCW = {
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = GRW_talk_with_MCW_idea_MCW_1
						add_idea = GRW_talk_with_MCW_idea_MCW_2
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GRW_talk_with_MCW_idea1
					add_idea = GRW_talk_with_MCW_idea2
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = generic_skip_one_line_tt
			GRW_primitive_communism_influence_slightincrease = yes
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = GRW_talk_with_MCW_idea2
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GRW_talk_with_MCW_idea2
					add_idea = GRW_talk_with_MCW_idea3
				}
				MCW = {
					swap_ideas = {

				}

						remove_idea = GRW_talk_with_MCW_idea_MCW_3
						add_idea = GRW_talk_with_MCW_idea_MCW_4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

				}
			}

			}

				fascism = 11
				communism = 65
				neutrality = 13
			}
			complete_national_focus = RCT_revolution_triumphant
		}
	}

	x = 1
	y = 1
	completion_reward = { 
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus GRW_Ninth_Column"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Arms Against Tyranny"
			}
			add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
				cost_reduction = 0.5
				name = GRW_Ninth_Column
				uses = 2
				category = cat_paratroopers_doctrine
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = GRW_Ninth_Column
				bonus = 1
				uses = 1
				category = para_tech
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = GRW_Ninth_Column
				bonus = 3
				uses = 1
				category = para_tech
			}
		}
	}
}
